  • ⚠️ $.facilityUse.aggregateFacilityUse.location.openingHoursSpecification: Recommended property openingHoursSpecification is missing from Place.
  • ⚠️ $.facilityUse.aggregateFacilityUse.provider.url: Recommended property url is missing from Organization.
  • ⚠️ $.facilityUse.aggregateFacilityUse.provider.telephone: Recommended property telephone is missing from Organization.
  • ⚠️ $.facilityUse.aggregateFacilityUse.provider.sameAs: Recommended property sameAs is missing from Organization.
  • ⚠️ $.offers[0].name: Recommended property name is missing from Offer.
  • ⚠️ $.offers[0].ageRestriction: Recommended property ageRestriction is missing from Offer.
